<p class="description">British retirees travel to India to take up residence in what they believe is a newly restored hotel.</p>
<p class="score"> Margaret: <img alt="three-and-a-half stars" class="rating" src="/web/20141229140508im_/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/img/stars-three-and-a-half.png"/> David: <img alt="three stars" class="rating" src="/web/20141229140508im_/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/img/stars-three.png"/> </p>

<div id="theReview">
<h2>The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel</h2>
<p class="ratd"> Rated <em>PG</em></p>
<p><em>Review by Margaret Pomeranz</em></p>
<p>It seems that retirees can't afford to live in Britain any more so old age is being outsourced to India, to THE BEST EXOTIC MARIGOLD HOTEL in Jaipur. It may sound glamorous but to the busload of disgruntled oldies from Britain it is a major disappointment. They are stubborn prejudiced Muriel, MAGGIE SMITH - who needs a hip replacement, mismatched married couple Douglas, BILL NIGHY and Jean, PENELOPE WILTON, recent widow Evelyn, JUDI DENCH, Graham, TOM WILKINSON, who grew up in India and has past issues to deal with, good-time girl Madge, CELIA IMRIE who's looking for a rich husband, and Norman, an inveterate ladies' man who's actually just looking for romance. Each responds to this strange, colourful new world in different ways.<br/><br/>The young owner of the hotel, DEV PATEL, is defying his family in keeping on with this inherited white elephant and in wanting to marry the girl he loves. <br/><br/>Ol Parker's screenplay opts for the obvious, although there are some delicious lines. I loved Maggie Smith's character being so pessimistic about her longevity she no longer buys green bananas. The pluses in the film, under John Madden's direction, are the setting and the cast. The Indian Tourist Board will love this film, it is India at its most colourful, Rajasthan is an amazing state. And to see this gathering of fine British talent strut their stuff is totally enjoyable. They are all so fine. Even though the manipulations at work here are just a touch too twee and predictable, The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel is one of those comfort zone films that is very easy to like</p>
<h2>Further comments</h2>
<p>MARGARET: David?<br/><br/>DAVID: Well, I agree with everything you've say, Margaret, on this.<br/><br/>MARGARET: That's rare.<br/><br/>DAVID: It is rare. The setting is marvellous and it's really lovely to see how well used it is. The cast is impeccable, all these terrific British character actors: Maggie Smith, Judi Dench, Bill Nighy, Tom Wilkinson. they're all very good. It's a pity that most of the best lines are in the trailer, so if you've seen the trailer, a lot of the jokes, you know them already, but it's an even greater pity that John Madden, who made SHAKESPEARE IN LOVE, does such an obvious job with it. Given the cast and given the setting it's a shame the film doesn't go in any really interesting directions. It's very predictable.<br/><br/>MARGARET: I blame Ol Parker. I think it's too easy to blame the director for this one.<br/><br/>DAVID: Well, yes. Well, the director surely had some say in the way the film is developed.<br/><br/>MARGARET: But did you feel that Maggie Smith's character was really a caricature rather than...<br/><br/>DAVID: It borders on that, I think, yes.<br/><br/>MARGARET: Oh, , ...<br/><br/>DAVID: Yes. I think she does it really well but I think it is, ...<br/><br/>MARGARET: She just eats it for breakfast, in large chunks. <br/><br/>DAVID: Well, yes. <br/><br/>MARGARET: I'm giving it three and a half stars. It's actually, a very pleasant film experience, not a great one.<br/><br/>DAVID: Exactly but I'm giving it three.<br/></p>

<p class="comment">((The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel))[[7]]<br>The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel nicely blends ripping one-liners and an array of seasoned characters with touches of sentiment throughout each of their stories. <p class="comment">((The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel))[[8]]<br>I resisted seeing thismovie; thought I'd hate it, but I really enjoyed it.<br>A huge plot contrivance is required at the beginning to get this disparate group of people together in India, but once they are there it is easy to sit back and enjoy watching these great old troopers do their stuff.<br>To say that all the best lines are in the trailer sells it short as there are  interesting plot developments as characters develop in their new environment.<br>That said, I'm not about to head for India because there is absolutely nothing believable about it.<br>Enjoyable nonsense, none the less. <br/></br></br></br></br></br></p>

<h3>Alistair :</h3>
<p class="date">22 Apr 2012 2:01:55am</p>
<p class="comment">((The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel))[[7]]<br>Beautiful movie, but thinking about it afterwards, a certain irony may have been lost on the writers. While these elderly Westerners fretted over lost opportunity, they are waited upon by the lowest of Indian castes, to whom opportunity is a dream.<br><br>So if you only focus only on the main characters, it's a lovely movie about embracing change. But if you consider the setting and lives around them, their concerns seem petty and ungracious.<br><br>This made the movie confusing.. I wanted to buy into the message, but felt vaguely ashamed doing so.<br/></br></br></br></br></br></p>

<h3>Nicholas :</h3>
<p class="date">09 Apr 2012 4:52:02pm</p>
<p class="comment">((The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel))[[5]]<br/>Great cast. Great setting. Mediocre script. Thoroughly predictable. Neglected a lot of the 'cultural' shock that would have injected some comedic interludes. These are retired English people and yet they accepted the heat, humidity, poverty, language, culture, smells and food of India without batting their colonial eyelids.What happened to Maggie Smith's character? She didn't want to let an Indian doctor get anywhere near her in England, but all her prejudices were for the most part unexplored in India as she went silently, quickly, and unobserved for her hip replacement in an Indian hospital..</p>

<p class="comment">((The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel))[[6]]<br/>Going against most people with this.  After a great start, when I thought I was going to be watching a great film, I thought it fell flat after about 45 minutes.  However, great mainly British stars did give it their all. <h3>ParryM :</h3>
<p class="date">25 Mar 2012 6:50:43am</p>
<p class="comment">((The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel))[[10]]<br/>David and Margaret, too much intellectualising! In saying all the funniest bits are in the trailers simply isn't true. I laughed all the way through and the subtlety is in small things and scenes throughout. I do however think it helps enormously to have been to and experienced  India first hand and to understand some Indian culture, because to some it may seem impossible to be actually like that, BUT it is! The colour, the sounds, the people, the dust! Our audience clapped at the end, but it was definitely mostly over fifty. Wonderful  uplifting movie. Go see it!</p>

<h3>Nicole :</h3>
<p class="date">24 Mar 2012 9:25:23pm</p>
<p class="comment">((The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel))[[10]]<br/>I loved this movie. I thought it had a great balance of humour, moments of poignancy and symbolism and some terrific one-liners. I found any elements of predictability just made it enjoyable to watch. I have worked in aged care, so many of the humourous references to ageing I found funny, even as a 30-something. The cast was great, the scenery gorgeous and I'll be watching it again.</p>

<a id="m_ucMessageDisplay13985_m_anchMessageAnchor" name="m13985"></a>
<h3>Thakur of Asind :</h3>
<p class="date">24 Mar 2012 8:42:00pm</p>
<p class="comment">((The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel))[[10]]<br/>We have been travelling to India of over 30 years on a regular basis. The film captures through European eyes and sensibilities, an enchanting segment of India. The script is tight and frequently incisive. Some of the characters e.g. the retired judge, are very well developed. He had the patina of "Old Filth" in Jane Gardam's wonderful novel.<br/>Sadly, I think neither David or Margaret have the ability to shed their middle class cocoon to enable them to enjoy the life offered by another culture so different to their own.</p>
<p class="links">
<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20141229140508/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/AlertModerator.aspx?b=117&amp;m=13985&amp;tpa=&amp;r=%2ftmb%2fView%2fMessage.aspx%3fb%3d117%26t%3d463%26a%3d0%26ps%3d50%26tpa%3d%26uto%3d1%26dm%3d4%26ci%3d0%26pd%3d1%26so%3dDateTime%26soa%3dFalse%26p%3d1%26p2%3d0" onclick="return popup(this.href);">Alert moderator</a>

<a id="m_ucMessageDisplay13957_m_anchMessageAnchor" name="m13957"></a>
<h3>goodstroke :</h3>
<p class="date">24 Mar 2012 6:31:28am</p>
<p class="comment">((The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel))[[10]]<br/>This is a film that overflows with  humanity and challenges even the jaded amongst us to embrace it with our senses not our intellect. It is a  stunningly beautiful visual feast as the camera alternately caresses the aged weathered surfaces of India and equally the skin of these National Treasures who explore the realities of growing old . It is predictable, like comfortable much loved jumpers, as welcome as the burst of  flavour of favourite fruit. The characters may be cliched- as are those of  Shakespeare and  of Dylan Thomas's "Under Milkwood". They are a mirror to ourselves.</p>
<p class="links">
<a href="https://web.archive.org/web/20141229140508/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/AlertModerator.aspx?b=117&amp;m=13957&amp;tpa=&amp;r=%2ftmb%2fView%2fMessage.aspx%3fb%3d117%26t%3d463%26a%3d0%26ps%3d50%26tpa%3d%26uto%3d1%26dm%3d4%26ci%3d0%26pd%3d1%26so%3dDateTime%26soa%3dFalse%26p%3d1%26p2%3d0" onclick="return popup(this.href);">Alert moderator</a>

$(document).ready(function(){

	
	$("#btnMobileMenu").click(function() {
		$("#mobileMenu").slideToggle('fast');
		$("#btnMobileMenu").toggleClass("buttonOn");
		dcsMultiTrack('DCS.dcsuri', 'ATM Mobile Menu Button', 'WT.ti', 'At the Movies Nav', 'WT.dl', '99');
		return false;
	});		
	
	$("#finda").focus(function() {
		$("body").scrollTo('#finda',1000);
		return false;
	});		
	
	$('#finda').autocomplete({
		lookup: movies,
		lookupLimit: 10,
		minChars:1,
		triggerSelectOnValidInput: false,
		onSelect: function (suggestion) {
			window.location = '/atthemovies/txt/'+suggestion.data+'.htm';
		}
	});	
	

	
	
// end ready
});

<script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">


var newtopicKey;

$(document).ready(function(){

audShow();
changeAction();
formatComments();

// end ready
});	

function audShow() {
	// display word count only if js enabled
	document.getElementById("wordCount").style.display='inline';
	document.getElementById("audiencecomment").style.display='block';
	if (document.getElementById("allnewComments")) {
		document.getElementById("allnewComments").innerHTML = document.getElementById("loadComments").innerHTML;
	}
}


function changeAction() {
	// avoids non-js form submission 
	var tmpStoryid = "??StoryID??";
	if (document.m_frmMainForm) {
		document.m_frmMainForm.action = 'https://web.archive.org/web/20141229140508/http://www2b.abc.net.au/tmb/View/NewMessage.aspx?b=117&amp;tn='+tmpStoryid+'&amp;dm=1&amp;tpa=&amp;r=&amp;layout=popup';
		}
}



function formatComments() {
	// replace H3 tag with 'Name:' + name
	var arrayH3 = document.getElementById("comments").getElementsByTagName("h3");
	for (var i = 0; i < arrayH3.length; i++) {
		var theString = arrayH3[i].innerHTML;
		theString = theString.replace(":", "");
		theString = "Name: "+theString;
		arrayH3[i].innerHTML = 	theString;
	}
	// add rating value to each comment
	var arrayComment = getElementsByClassName( 'comment', 'p' );	
	for (var c = 0; c < arrayComment.length; c++) {
		var theComment = arrayComment[c].innerHTML;
		theComment = theComment.replace("[[", "<span class='userRating'>Rating: <img src='https://web.archive.org/web/20141229140508/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/audience/stars").replace("]]",".png' alt='rating'></span>").replace("((", "<!-- ").replace(")))", "))").replace("))", "-->");
		arrayComment[c].innerHTML = theComment;
	}

	
}


function formCheck(zeForm) {
	// pass key to form
	document.getElementById("keyField").value = newtopicKey;
	// basic validation
	if (document.getElementById("yname").value.length < 1) {
		alert("Please enter your name or nickname.");
		document.getElementById("yname").style.background='#FFFDC8';
		return false;
	}
	if (document.getElementById("yemail").value.length < 6) {
		alert("Please enter a valid email address.");
		document.getElementById("yemail").style.background='#FFFDC8';
		return false;
	}
	if (zeForm.score.options[0].selected && zeForm.score.options[0].value=="na") {
		alert("You forgot to rate the movie!");
		document.getElementById("score").style.background='#FFFDC8';	
		return false;
	}	
	// check for http
	spamcheck=zeForm.m_tbxText.value;
	if (spamcheck.indexOf("http")!=-1) {
		document.m_frmMainForm.action = 'https://web.archive.org/web/20141229140508/http://www.abc.net.au/atthemovies/audience/blank.htm';
	}
	// check word count
	wct = cnt(zeForm.m_tbxText.value);
	if (wct > 100) {
		alert("Comments are limited to 100 words. You've written "+wct+" words!");
		document.getElementById("remark").style.background='#FFFDC8';
		return false;	
	}
	
	// replace usual suspect bad characters 
	badChars = Array  ('', '', '', '', '', 'ö', 'é', 'è', 'ñ', 'â', ' ', '','','´');
	goodChars = Array ('...', '-', '-', '"', '"', 'o', 'e', 'e', 'n', 'a', ' ', '\'','\'','\'');
	fld = document.getElementById("remark");
	for(i=0;i<badChars.length;i++){
		restring = new RegExp( badChars[i] , 'g');
		fld.value = fld.value.replace(restring,goodChars[i]);
	}
	fldn = document.getElementById("yname");
	for(j=0;j<badChars.length;j++){
		restringj = new RegExp( badChars[j] , 'g');
		fldn.value = fldn.value.replace(restringj,goodChars[j]);
	}	
	
	// add rating to comment field in [[ ]] tags 
	var theSel = zeForm.score.selectedIndex;
	var theRating = zeForm.score[theSel].value; 
	zeForm.m_tbxText.value = "[["+theRating+"]]\n" + zeForm.m_tbxText.value;
	
	// add movie title to comment field in (( )) tags 
	zeForm.m_tbxText.value = "(("+theMovie+"))" + zeForm.m_tbxText.value;	
	
	// display thankyou div layer and hide form. 
	document.getElementById("favFormThx").style.display='block';
	document.getElementById("favForm").style.display='none';
	document.getElementById("wordCount").style.display='none';	
	
	// all clear, submit the form
	return true;
}

// word count function
function cnt(theform){
	var y=theform;
	var r = 0;
	a=y.replace('\n',' ');
	a=a.split(' ');
	for (z=0; z<a.length; z++) {if (a[z].length > 0) r++;}
	return r;
}

function remainingWords(textAreaContent,textAreaContentValue, maxWords) 
{
	// Determine the number of words we have left
	var numberofwords = cnt(textAreaContentValue);
	wordsLeft = maxWords - numberofwords;
	if (wordsLeft < 1)
	{	// if 100 change color to red
		document.getElementById("wcNum").style.color='red'; 
	} else {
		document.getElementById("wcNum").style.color='#ffffff'; 
	}
	// update word count number
	document.getElementById("wcNum").innerHTML=(0+numberofwords);
}

// windows media alt box
function showWindows() {
	document.getElementById("windowsMed").style.display='block';
}


// generic get by class name
function getElementsByClassName(strClass, strTag, objContElm) {
  strTag = strTag || "*";
  objContElm = objContElm || document;    
  var objColl = objContElm.getElementsByTagName(strTag);
  if (!objColl.length &&  strTag == "*" &&  objContElm.all) objColl = objContElm.all;
  var arr = new Array();                              
  var delim = strClass.indexOf('|') != -1  ? '|' : ' ';   
  var arrClass = strClass.split(delim);    
  for (var i = 0, j = objColl.length; i < j; i++) {                         
    var arrObjClass = objColl[i].className.split(' ');   
    if (delim == ' ' && arrClass.length > arrObjClass.length) continue;
    var c = 0;
    comparisonLoop:
    for (var k = 0, l = arrObjClass.length; k < l; k++) {
      for (var m = 0, n = arrClass.length; m < n; m++) {
        if (arrClass[m] == arrObjClass[k]) c++;
        if ((delim == '|' && c == 1) || (delim == ' ' && c == arrClass.length)) {
          arr.push(objColl[i]); 
          break comparisonLoop;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return arr; 
}

// called from 'new discussion' page in iframe
function sayHello(theKey) {
	newtopicKey = theKey;
}

// talk to www2b iframe
document.domain = "abc.net.au";

</script>

		//mobile device supports m3u8 html5 HLS video	
		$('#flashplayer').html('<img id="playerNew" src="/atthemovies/img/2012/ep07/marigold_large.jpg" width="598" height="336" alt="The Best Exotic Marigold Hotel" />Video clips on this site prior to June 2012 do not play on mobile devices.');
	}
	else {
		//desktop browsers flash
		cinerama.highlightColour = "#006CD9";
		cinerama.playlistType = "horizontal"
		cinerama.embedPlayer('playerNew','rtmp://cp44823.edgefcs.net/ondemand/flash/tv/streams/atthemovies/20120321_marigoldhotel_hi.flv',598,336,'',false);
	} 	
			
	
// end ready
});
